August 16, 2006

Descendants of Per Henriksson and Anna Mårtensdotter

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Per Henriksson and Anna Mårtensdotter.
Per and Anna were one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
You may with to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute new information.

August 07, 2006

Descendants of Frederick and Mary Brinker

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Frederick and Mary Brinker.
Frederick Mary Brinker are not one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
Their parents would be part of the sixteen sets. I know little about Frederick Mary.
Their child John Charles Brinker was extremely secretive about his past; and when he did speak of his birth and parents, he sometimes provided contradictory information. He found it difficult to keep his story straight. The name of his parents was provided on his first marriage license. The last name of his mother was found on his death certificate and was like provided by his son. I do believe that John was born in Pennsyvania and I have found a possible listing in the 1870 census for a boy that could be him. If it is him, he is not living with his parents or his parents are not Frederick and Mary.
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute new information.

August 05, 2006

Descendants of Heinrich and Anna Koch

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Heinrich and Anna Koch.
Heinrich and Anna were one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
I do not have not listed all of their children, because I have not yet discovered their names.
I hope that one day I will learn them. Likely after a journey to a German archive.
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of descendants.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute new information.

August 04, 2006

Descendants of John and Martha Porter

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of John and Martha Porter.
John and Martha were one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
I do not have not listed all of their children, because I have not yet discovered their names.
I hope that one day I will learn them
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants.
At this link you will find more than 50 generations of ancestors for Martha, and sixteen generations for John.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute information.

August 03, 2006

Descendants of Benjamin Tupper and Irene Simmons

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Benjamin Foster Tupper and his two wives: Amelia B. Randall and Irene Simmons.
Benjamin and Irene were one of my sixteen sets of my great great great grandparents.
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants.
At this link you will find more than 50 generations of ancestors for Benjamin, but I only know the names of Irene's parents.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute information.

August 02, 2006

Descendants of Horace and Althea Wright

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Horace and Althea Wright.
Horace and Althea were one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants. At this link you will find more than 50 generations of ancestors for Horace and Althea.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute information.

Descendants of Zenas and Nancy Miller

Nancy Partridge and Zenas Miller

If you have found this page, then you were looking for a common relative.
The listing below contains the descendants of Zenas and Nancy Miller.
Zenas and Nacy were one of my sixteen sets of my great-great-great grandparents.
You may wish to visit my family tree index for a complete listing of both ancestors and descendants. At this link you will find more than 50 generations of ancestors for Zenas and Nancy.
Contact me, if you find an error that you want corrected or if you want to contribute information.
